\DoxyCodeLine{83 \textcolor{comment}{// MatrixProduct decomposes real/imaginary vectors into a real vector and an imaginary vector, this turned out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{84 \textcolor{comment}{// to be faster than Eigen's usual approach of having real/imaginary pairs on a single vector. This constants then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{85 \textcolor{comment}{// are responsible to extract from convert between Eigen's and MatrixProduct approach.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86 }
\DoxyCodeLine{87 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{static} Packet16uc p16uc\_GETREAL32 = \{  0,  1,  2,  3,}
\DoxyCodeLine{88                                              8,  9, 10, 11,}
\DoxyCodeLine{89                                             16, 17, 18, 19,}
\DoxyCodeLine{90                                             24, 25, 26, 27\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{91 }
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{static} Packet16uc p16uc\_GETIMAG32 = \{  4,  5,  6,  7,}
\DoxyCodeLine{93                                             12, 13, 14, 15,}
\DoxyCodeLine{94                                             20, 21, 22, 23,}
\DoxyCodeLine{95                                             28, 29, 30, 31\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{static} Packet16uc p16uc\_GETREAL64 = \{  0,  1,  2,  3,  4,  5,  6,  7,}
\DoxyCodeLine{97                                             16, 17, 18, 19, 20, 21, 22, 23\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 }
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{//[a,ai],[b,bi] = [ai,bi]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{static} Packet16uc p16uc\_GETIMAG64 = \{  8,  9, 10, 11, 12, 13, 14, 15,}
\DoxyCodeLine{101                                             24, 25, 26, 27, 28, 29, 30, 31\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 }
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{/*********************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{ * Single precision real and complex packing *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{ * *******************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 }
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Scalar, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} Index, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} StorageOrder>}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 EIGEN\_ALWAYS\_INLINE std::complex<Scalar> getAdjointVal(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} j, const\_blas\_data\_mapper<std::complex<Scalar>, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}, StorageOrder>\& dt)}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{124   std::complex<Scalar> v;}
\DoxyCodeLine{125   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(i < j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{126   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{127     v.real( dt(j,i).real());}
\DoxyCodeLine{128     v.imag(-\/dt(j,i).imag());}
\DoxyCodeLine{129   \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(i > j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{130   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{131     v.real( dt(i,j).real());}
\DoxyCodeLine{132     v.imag( dt(i,j).imag());}
\DoxyCodeLine{133   \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{134     v.real( dt(i,j).real());}
\DoxyCodeLine{135     v.imag((Scalar)0.0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{136   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} v;}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 }
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Scalar, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} Index, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} StorageOrder, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} N>}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} symm\_pack\_complex\_rhs\_helper(std::complex<Scalar>* blockB, \textcolor{keyword}{const} std::complex<Scalar>* \_rhs, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} rhsStride, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} rows, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} cols, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{143   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} depth = k2 + rows;}
\DoxyCodeLine{144   const\_blas\_data\_mapper<std::complex<Scalar>, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}, StorageOrder> rhs(\_rhs, rhsStride);}
\DoxyCodeLine{145   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} vectorSize = N*quad\_traits<Scalar>::vectorsize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{146   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} vectorDelta = vectorSize * rows;}
\DoxyCodeLine{147   Scalar* blockBf = \textcolor{keyword}{reinterpret\_cast<}Scalar *\textcolor{keyword}{>}(blockB);}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 }
\DoxyCodeLine{149   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} rir = 0, rii, j = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{150   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; j + vectorSize <= cols; j+=vectorSize)}
\DoxyCodeLine{151   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{152     rii = rir + vectorDelta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 }
\DoxyCodeLine{154     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i = k2; i < depth; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{155     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{156       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k = 0; k < vectorSize; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{157       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{158         std::complex<Scalar> v = getAdjointVal<Scalar, Index, StorageOrder>(i, j + k, rhs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 }
\DoxyCodeLine{160         blockBf[rir + k] = v.real();}
\DoxyCodeLine{161         blockBf[rii + k] = v.imag();}
\DoxyCodeLine{162       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163       rir += vectorSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{164       rii += vectorSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{165     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166 }
\DoxyCodeLine{167     rir += vectorDelta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{168   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j < cols)}
\DoxyCodeLine{170   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{171     rii = rir + ((cols -\/ j) * rows);}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 }
\DoxyCodeLine{173     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i = k2; i < depth; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{174     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{175       \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k = j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{176       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; k < cols; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{177       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{178         std::complex<Scalar> v = getAdjointVal<Scalar, Index, StorageOrder>(i, k, rhs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 }
\DoxyCodeLine{180         blockBf[rir] = v.real();}
\DoxyCodeLine{181         blockBf[rii] = v.imag();}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 }
\DoxyCodeLine{183         rir += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{184         rii += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{185       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Scalar, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} Index, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} StorageOrder, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} N>}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} symm\_pack\_rhs\_helper(Scalar* blockB, \textcolor{keyword}{const} Scalar* \_rhs, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} rhsStride, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} rows, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} cols, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{244   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} depth = k2 + rows;}
\DoxyCodeLine{245   const\_blas\_data\_mapper<Scalar, Index, StorageOrder> rhs(\_rhs, rhsStride);}
\DoxyCodeLine{246   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} vectorSize = quad\_traits<Scalar>::vectorsize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 }
\DoxyCodeLine{248   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} ri = 0, j = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{249   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; j + N*vectorSize <= cols; j+=N*vectorSize)}
\DoxyCodeLine{250   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{251     \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i = k2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{252     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; i < depth; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{253     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{254       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k = 0; k < N*vectorSize; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{255       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{256         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(i <= j+k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{257           blockB[ri + k] = rhs(j+k, i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{258         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259           blockB[ri + k] = rhs(i, j+k);}
\DoxyCodeLine{260       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261       ri += N*vectorSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{262     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 }
\DoxyCodeLine{265   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j < cols)}
\DoxyCodeLine{266   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{267     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i = k2; i < depth; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{268     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{269       \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k = j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{270       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; k < cols; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{271       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{272         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(k <= i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{273           blockB[ri] = rhs(i, k);}
\DoxyCodeLine{274         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275           blockB[ri] = rhs(k, i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{276         ri += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{277       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Scalar, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} Index, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} StorageOrder>}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} symm\_pack\_lhs\_helper(Scalar* blockA, \textcolor{keyword}{const} Scalar* \_lhs, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} lhsStride, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} cols, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} rows)}

\DoxyCodeLine{287   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} vectorSize = quad\_traits<Scalar>::vectorsize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{288 }
\DoxyCodeLine{289   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} ri = 0, j = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{290   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; j + vectorSize <= rows; j+=vectorSize)}
\DoxyCodeLine{291   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{292     \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{293 }
\DoxyCodeLine{294     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; i < depth; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{295     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{296       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k = 0; k < vectorSize; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{297       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{298         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(i <= j+k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{299           blockA[ri + k] = lhs(j+k, i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{300         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{301           blockA[ri + k] = lhs(i, j+k);}
\DoxyCodeLine{302       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{303       ri += vectorSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{304     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{305   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{306 }
\DoxyCodeLine{307   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j < rows)}
\DoxyCodeLine{308   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{309     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i = 0; i < depth; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{310     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{311       \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k = j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{312       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; k < rows; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{313       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{314         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(i <= k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{315           blockA[ri] = lhs(k, i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{316         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317           blockA[ri] = lhs(i, k);}
\DoxyCodeLine{318         ri += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{319       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321   \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{539     \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{541       rii = rir + (((PanelMode) ? stride : depth) * (rows -\/ j));}
\DoxyCodeLine{542 }
\DoxyCodeLine{543       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} i = 0; i < depth; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{544       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{545         \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} k = j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{546         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(; k < rows; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{547         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{548           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (UseLhs) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{549             blockAt[rir] = lhs(k, i).real();}
\DoxyCodeLine{550 }
\DoxyCodeLine{551             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Conjugate}{Conjugate}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{552               blockAt[rii] = -\/lhs(k, i).imag();}
\DoxyCodeLine{553             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{554               blockAt[rii] =  lhs(k, i).imag();}
\DoxyCodeLine{555           \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{556             blockAt[rir] = lhs(i, k).real();}
\DoxyCodeLine{557 }
\DoxyCodeLine{558             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Conjugate}{Conjugate}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{559               blockAt[rii] = -\/lhs(i, k).imag();}
\DoxyCodeLine{560             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{561               blockAt[rii] =  lhs(i, k).imag();}
\DoxyCodeLine{562           \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{563 }
\DoxyCodeLine{564           rir += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{565           rii += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{566         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{567       \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2319 EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} gemm\_complex(\textcolor{keyword}{const} DataMapper\& res, \textcolor{keyword}{const} LhsScalar* blockAc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} RhsScalar* blockBc, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} rows, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} depth, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} cols, Scalarc alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} strideA, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} strideB, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} offsetA, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} offsetB)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2322       \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} remaining\_cols = cols \% accRows;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2323 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2324       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( strideA == -\/1 ) strideA = depth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2325       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( strideB == -\/1 ) strideB = depth;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2337         \textcolor{keyword}{const} Scalar* rhs\_base = blockB + advanceCols*col*strideB + accRows*offsetB;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2338         \textcolor{keyword}{const} Scalar* lhs\_base = blockA;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2339         \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} row = 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2344         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2345         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch}( (rows-\/row)/accCols ) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2347           \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4:}
